 The much awaited 'humsafar Express' train will start from New Delhi on Friday
 kai suvidhaon se yukt is train ke liye flixi kiraaya lagu hoga
 Flexi fair system means increasing fares with decreasing seats
 isamen sabhi coach asi-3 honge
 Since this train is equipped with coffee, tea, soup vending machines and each cabin has a refrigerated pantry and other facilities, the passengers are charged 1 as base fare as against the normal mail, express AC-3
 15 fisadi adhik kiraaya dena hoga
 According to a senior railway officer, the cost of manufacturing of these coaches with modern facility is higher as compared to the normal AC coaches
 aise main special fares rakhe gaye hai
 Railway Minister Suresh Prabhu will inaugurate the full AC-3 service between gorakhpur-anand Vihar through video conferencing
 gauratlab he ki beete saal rail bajet main rail mantri suresh prabhu ne humsafar train kaa elaan kiya tha
 All coaches will be in the AC-3 category
 isamen sisitivi, jeepies-besd paisangers information system, fire or smoke ditection or sapressant system rahegaa
 Humsafar coaches will be like the coaches of Maharaja Express
 chunki yah train coffee, chaay, soup vending mashin se yukt he or prayek cabin main refriorated pentry tathaa anya suvidhaayen maujuud hai, isliye yatriyon ko saamaanya mail, express asi-3 ke mukaable aadhaar kiraye ke taur par 1
 15% higher rent will have to be paid
 ek senior railway afasar ke mutabik, normal AC kochon kii tulana main modern facelity vaale in kochon kii nirmaan laagat zyada he
 In this case, special fairs are kept
 railmantri suresh prabhu video conferencing ke jariye gorakhpur-anand vihaar ke bich purna asi-3 seva kaa udghaatan karenge
 It is worth noting that in the Railway Budget last year, Railway Minister Suresh Prabhu announced Humsafar Train
 isamen sabhi coach asi-3 category ke honge
 It will have CCTV, gps-based passenger information system, fire and smoke detection and suppression system

 ) Cases of useless use of red light keep coming up
 lekin ab kendriya parivahan mantri nitin gadakari ne laal battiyon ke upyog ko behad simit karne kaa prastaav diya he
 In this proposal, Gadkari said that only five constitutional dignitaries from the Center and four people from the states should be given red lights
 gadakari ne antim prastaav se pehle apane mantriyon ko is par apana paksh rakhane ko kaha he
 Gadkari has advocated that the facility of red light at the center should be provided only to the President, Vice President, Prime Minister, Chief Justice of the Supreme Court and Speaker of the Lok Sabha, whereas in the states, this facility will be provided with the Chief Minister, Governor, Chief Justice of the High Court Be given only to the speaker of the assembly
 gadakari ne likhit main ye prastaav apane kai kendriya mantriyon ko bheja he
 These ministers also include Rajnath Singh, Arun Jaitley, Sushma Swaraj
 gadakari ne vibhinn mantralayon main is prastaav ko raishumaari ke liye bhej diya he
 This proposal will be placed before the government only when the Chief Minister will put his opinion on it

 but my fight against drug mafia and all kind of corruption in Punjab will continue as an “aam Aadmi “ of Punjab - Bhagwant Mann (@bhagwantmann) March 16, 2018 bataa den ki arvind kejariwal kii aam aadmi party, jiske netaaon par 20 se zyada manahani ke maamle darj hai, ne un maamalon ko nipataane kaa faisla kiya he
 Kejriwal will talk to all concerned leaders to end all defamation cases going on
 arun jetali, nitin gadakari samet kai netaaon ne kejariwal par manahani ke mukademe kar rakhe hai
 According to Delhi government sources, CM Kejriwal has to waste hours in court every day which is affecting his functioning
 isliye ab sabhi mukademe khatm karne ke liye koshish karenge
 The comments padhein :arvind kejariwal ke bayaan se AAP saansad sanjay singh ne kiya kinaaraa, bole - main bayaan par kaayam Kejriwal wrote in an apology letter to Akali Dal leader Majithia, 'now i know that all the allegations are baseless, so i withdraw all the allegations and statements made against you and also apologize for them
 ' Let me tell you that in May last year, Arvind Kejriwal, surrounded by Kapil Mishra's allegations, took a big decision and appointed Bhagwant Mann as the convener of Punjab
 tab arvind kejariwal ne bhagwant maan ko sharaab pine par kaabo rakhane kii baat bhi kahi thi
 Let me tell you that the MP Bhagwant Mann has created chaos many times by drinking alcohol and he has been accused of going to the Parliament too
 kai saansadon ne loksabhaa spikar se is baat kii shikaayat bhi kii thi
 In response, Majithia sued Arvind Kejriwal for defamation
 yah mukadmaa chal rahaa tha
 Now Kejriwal has accepted that there was no basis for his allegations
 vah iske liye maafee maangate hai or cese ko waapas lene kii apil bhi kii he

 unhone kaha, ek baar kar rajasav badhane par ek saal baad hamen adhibhaar kii jarurat nahin hogi

 He said the surcharge would not lead to tax evasion

 The Finance Minister said that he will answer all the criticisms regarding the budget as anti-people and anti-farmer

 He described the current current account deficit as a complex issue, as imports are much higher than exports

 vahiin maharashtra main 56

 mumbai dakshin loksabhaa seat par 13 ummidavaar kismat aajamaa rahe hai

 vahiin congress kii ore se milind devda maidan main hai

 is seat se kabhi jorge furnandis saansad bane the
 He was a 9-time MP
 baad main unhone bihar kii mujffarpur seat ko apni karmasthali banaaya
 For many years, this seat remained with Congress's Murali Deora and then his son, Milind Deora, but later it went to Shiv Sena's account
 yahaan se vartmaan saansad shivasena ke arvind saavant hai jinhone congress ke milind devda ko shikast di thi
 The history of the seat was held by the Congress from 1952 to 1967 here
 sanyukt socialist party ke binar par lade jorge furnandis ne congress ke tilism ko todaa or 1967 ke chunaavon main jeet hasil kii
 The seat again went to the Congress in 1971
 1977 se 1984 tak ye seat bhartiya lok dal or janata party ke paas rahi
 After that from 1984 to 1996, Congress's Murali Deora ruled uninterrupted
 1996 main unke tilism ko bijepi kii jaivantiben mehta ne todaa, lekin 1998 main phir se murali devda ko yahaan se jeet hasil hui
 In 1999, Jayawantiben Mehta won again
